climat chang by geoffrey lean nuclear power can not solv global warming the international body set up to promot atomic energy admits today the international atomic energy agency iaea which exists to spread the peaceful use of the atom reveals in a new report that it could not grow fast enough over the next decades to slow climat chang eve under the most favorabl circumstances the report published to celebrat yesterday anniversary of nuclear power contradicts a recent surg of support for the atom as the answer to global warming that surg was provoked by an articl in the independent last month by professor james lovelock the creator of the gaia theory who said that only a massiv expansio of nuclear power as the world main energy sourc could prevent climat chang overwhelming the globe professor lovelock a nuclear supporter wrote civilizatio is in imminent danger and has to use nuclear the one safe availabl energy sourc now or suffer the pain soon to be inflicted by our outraged plane his comments were backed by sir bernard ingham lady thatcher former pr chief and other commentators but have now been rebutted by the most authoritativ organizatio the matter unlik fossil fuels nuclear power emits no carbo dioxid the main cause of climat chang however it has long been in decl in the face of rising public oppositio and increasing reluctanc of governments and utilities to financ its enormous constructio costs no new atomic power statio has been ordered in the us for a quarter of a century and only one is being built in wester europ in finland meanwhil germany belgium the netherlands and swede have al pledged to phase out existing plants the iaea report considers two scenarios in the first nuclear energy continues to decl with no new stations built beyond those already planned its share of world electricity and thus its relativ contributio to fighting global warming drops from its current per cent to per cent by surprisingly it made an eve smaller relativ contributio to combating climat chang under the iaea most favorabl scenario seeing nuclear power grow by per cent over the next years this is becaus the world would have to be so prosperous to afford the expansions that traditional ways of generating electricity from fossil fuels would have grow eve faster climat chang would doom the plane befor nuclear power could save it ala mcdonald an iaea nuclear energy analyst told the independent sunday last night saying that nuclear power can solv global warming by itself is way over the top but added that closing existing nuclear power stations would make tackling climat chang harder © independent digital uk ltd

johdo valmistaj päätyi lähettäm minu kenkäpar sija on suunnittelu materiaalivalino tuotetestauks otetu riittäv huomio todellis talviolosuht ensin pakkas vaikutus materiaalivalinto väitä otetu huomio valmistuskustannuks painav vaakakup laadu kustannuks muistut suome lap oike talv pak tunnetu kuoma keng istuv suomais jalk tarp leveä lest johdo minu jalk kuoma kari istuiv tosi suosittel seisoskelu pyörätuol käyttäv siirtymis kävel tarkoitus käyt talvikel näih tarkoituks varm järkev ost kolmenky halpiskeng viite tun vastu sano jalkin tekev kuomiokosk oy n toimitusjohtaj ant putton van sanom edel viite tulk jalkin kest normaalikäytö kokemu kuoma kari kenkäpar kes käytö talvikäytö kenkäpar kest kalenterivuod ote huomio talvikenk käyte kesä siis talv kulu lopu kuoma kari kenkäpar käytö tunt kävely viiko minu yllätys pettymys mielikuv kotimaist kenk korkea laadu myyt nyt myyt murtui sortui korttitalo en os jalkin ” taku ” tuotevastu johdo saa valmistaj käytettäväks kenkäpar hin kuomiokosk oy pesy käte asia se antanu vastau vastauspyyntöih kosk kenkäpar rikkoontum lyhye tarkoitai kolmat kenkäpar hin neljät sitten… jne ” hyvä kelo kauas kuulu paha ”
